 His first home production film was 'chhote Nawab'
 unhone bataur nirdeshak suspence-kamedi film 'bhoot bangla' banaai
 Mahmood, who worked as an actor, director, narrator and producer, made his last film 'dushman Duniya Ka' in 1996 with Shah Rukh Khan, but failed at the box office
 apni chhavi main ai ekarupata se bachane ke liye mahmud ne apane aap ko vibhinn prakaar kii bhoomikaaon main pesh kiya
 In the same sequence, in the year 1968, the name of the film 'padosan' comes first
 'padosan' main mahmud ne nakaaratmak bhoomika nibhaai or darshakon kii vaahvahee luutane main safal rahe
 'padosan' was a tremendous hit of the 60s
 'padosan' ko hindi cinema jagat kii shreshth hasya filmon main gina jaataa he
 He appeared heavily on the character of the hero in many of his films
 'padosan' main mahmud par filmaaya gaanaa 'ek chatur naar karke shringaar' kaaphi lokapriy hua
 In the 1970 film Humjoli, the audience got to see various forms of acting of Mahmood
 is film main mahmud ne tihari bhoomika nibhaai or darshakon kaa dhyaan apni ore khinchaa
 The comments mahmud ko apane sine kariyar main teen baar filmphere puraskaar se sammanit kiya gaya
 On 23 July 2004, Mahmud departed from this world forever and only his beautiful memories remain among us
 (is khabar ko enditivi team ne sampadit nahin kiya he
 It is published directly from the Syndicate feed
 ) In the language of Mahmud, the Hyderabadi style was liked by the audience and the great style of his speaking and acting made millions of people crazy
 mahmud ne jis vakt filmon ko gambhirtha se lenaa shuru kiya tha, us samay bhartiya film jagat main kishor kumaar kii kamedi kaa jaadu chaaya hua tha
 Writer Manmohan Melville has narrated an interesting anecdote of Mahmood and Kishore in one of his articles
 isamen kaha gaya he ki mahmud ne apane kariyar ke sunahare daur se guzar rahe kishor se apni kisi film main bhoomika dene kii guzarish kii thi, lekin mahmud kii pratibha se puri tarah waakif kishor ne kaha tha ki vah aise kisi vyakti ko mauka kaise de sakate hai, jo bhavishya main unheen ke liye chunauti ban jaae
 On this, Mahmud said with great humility that one day i will also become a big filmmaker and will give you a role in my film
 mahmud apni baat ke pakke sabit hue or aage chalakar jab unhone apni home production kii film 'padosan' shuru kii to usamen kishor ko kaam diya
 The film proved to be Bollywood's biggest comedy film due to the jugalbandi of both these great actors
 mahmud ke teen dashak lambey kariyar main 300 se zyada hindi filmein unke naam hai
 Mahmood was one of the eight children of actor and dance artist Mumtaz Ali
 abhinayta ke taur par kaam se pehle vah chote-mote kaam karte the, vaahan chalaane kaa kaam bhi karte the
 At that time, Meena Kumari was hired to teach table tennis
 baad main unhone minaa kumari kii bahan madhu se shaadi kii
 After marrying and becoming a father, he decided to pursue acting to earn more money
 shuruyaat main unhone 'do bigha jameen' or 'pyaasa' jaisi filmon main chote-mote kirdaar nibhaae
 Mehmood got his first big chance in films with 'parvarish' (1958)
 isamen unhone film ke nayak rajkpur ke bhai kaa kirdaar nibhaayaa tha or uske baad unhone film 'gumnaam' main bhi kaam kiya
 He gave hits like 'pyar Kiya Jaa', 'pyar Hi Pyar', 'sasural', 'love in Tokyo' and 'stubborn'
 iske baad unhone kuch filmon main mukhya bhoomika bhi nibhaai, lekin darshakon ne unhen ek kamedian ke taur par zyada pasand kiya
 Mahmud later opened his own production house
 unki pehali home production film 'chote nawab' thi
 He made the suspense-comedy film Bhoot Bangla as a director
 abhinayta, nirdeshak, kathakaar or nirmaataa ke rup main kaam karne vaale mahmud ne shahrukh khan ko lekar varsh 1996 main apni aakhri film 'dushman duniya kaa' banaai, lekin vah box offis par naakaam rahi
 To avoid uniformity in his image, Mahmood introduced himself in a wide variety of roles
 isi kram main varsh 1968 main film 'padosan' kaa naam sabase pehle aata he
 In 'padosan', Mahmood played a negative role and managed to rob the applause of the audience
 'padosan' 60 ke dashak kii jabardast hit sabit hui thi
 'padosan' is counted among the best comedy films of the Hindi cinema world
 apni anek filmon main vah nayak ke kirdaar par baari najar aae
 The song 'ek Chatur Nar Karkar Shringar', which was filmed on Mehmood in 'padosan', became very popular
 1970 main film 'hamajoli' main mahmud ke abhinay ke vividh rup darshakon ko dekhne ko mili
 In this film, Mahmood played a triple role and caught the attention of the audience
 tippaniyan Mehmood was awarded the Filmfare Award thrice in his cine career
 23 july, 2004 ko mahmud is duniya se hameshaa ke liye chale gaye or hamaare bich keval unki khubasurat yaaden hi baaki hai
 (this news has not been edited by the NDTV team
 yah syndicate feed se sidhe prakashit kii gai he
 ) lekhak manmohan melville ne apane ek lekh main mahmud or kishor ke dilachasp kisse ko bayaan kiya he
 It said that Mahmood had requested Kishore, who is going through the golden phase of his career, to play a role in one of his films, but Kishore, who was fully aware of Mahmood's talent, said that how can he give such a chance to someone Which will become a challenge for them in the future
 is par mahmud ne badi vinamrata ke saath kaha ki ek din main bhi bada filmkaar banuunga or aapako apni film main bhoomika duungaa
 Mehmood proved his point and later when he started his home production film 'padosan', he hired Kishore in it
 in donon mahaan kalakaaron kii jugalbandi se yah film bollywood kii sabase badi kamedi film sabit hui
 He has more than 300 Hindi films in Mahmood's three-decade long career
 mahmud abhinayta or nrity kalakaar mumtaj ali ke aath bacchon main se ek the
 Prior to his work as an actor, he used to do petty jobs, also driving vehicles
 us jamaane main minaa kumari ko teble tennis sikhaane ke liye unhen naukari par rakhaa gaya tha
 He later married Meena Kumari's sister Madhu
 shaadi karne or pita banane ke baad zyada paise kamaane ke liye unhone abhinay karne kaa nishchay kiya
 Initially, he played minor roles in films like 'do Bigha Zameen' and 'pyaasa'
 mahmud ko filmon main pehla bada mauka 'parvarish' (1958) se mila tha
 In this, he played the role of the brother of the film's hero Raj Kapoor and after that he also acted in the film 'gumnaam'
 unhone 'pyaar kiye ja', 'pyaar hi pyaar', 'sasuraal', 'lav in tokyo' or 'ziddee' jaisi hit filmein di
 He then went on to play the lead role in a few films, but the audience liked him more as a comedian
 mahmud ne baad main apana khud kaa production house kholaa

 'mere dream girl' and 'roop tera mastana'
 
 
 ’ jaise romantic geeton ke bhaavon ko apni jajbaati adaakaari se jeevant karne vaale rajesh khanna ne apane jamaane main lagaataar 15 hit filmein dekar baliwood ko ‘super star’ kii paribhaasha di thi
 The style of Rajesh Khanna's hair, or the way of dressup, their dialogue payoff or the effort to lightly tilt the eyelids, curl the neck and release the arrows of the eyes
 
 His every act was killer
 unki filmon ke ek ek romantic dialog par cinemagharon ke neem andhere main sitiyaan hi sitiyaan goonjati thi
 The 69-year-old Bollywood 'superstar' breathed his last at his home in Bandra, Mumbai
 rajesh khanna ko aise hi super star nahin kaha jaataa tha
 The young men and women were so fond of them that when they went to the markets, the girls kissed their car like crazy and the car was stained with lipstick
 yuvatiyaan unhen apane khun se likhe khat bheja karti thim
 Even before his star Raj Kapoor and Dilip Kumar, people were crazy, but there is no doubt that the madness that was meant for Rajesh Khanna was never seen before or after
 29 disambar 1942 ko rajesh khanna kaa janm amritsar main hua tha or unki parvarish unke dattak mata pita ne kii
 His name was Jatin Khanna earlier
 schuli dinon se hi rajesh khanna kaa jhukaav abhinay kii ore ho gaya tha or isi ke chalate unhone kai naatakon main abhinay bhi kiya
 When the age of dreaming came, Jatin decided to take the path of films
 yah daur unki jindagi kii nayi ibaarat likhakar laayaa or unke chachaa ne unka naam jatin se badal kar rajesh kar diya
 This name not only brought him fame, but this name became immortal in the mind of every young man and woman
 1965 main rajesh khanna ne united produrs and filmphere ke pratibha khoj abhiyaan main baaji maari or uske baad shoharat or daulat unke kadam chuumati chali gayi
 His first film was Aakhri Khat which was directed by Chetan Anand
 unhen duusari film mili ‘raaj’
 The film was also the prize for winning the competition
 us daur main dilip kumaar or raaj kapur ke abhinay kaa danka bajataa tha or kisi ko ahsaas bhi nahin tha ki ek ‘nayaa sitara’ shoharat ke aasmaan ko kabjane ke liye bad rahaa he
 Rajesh Khanna gave early successful films like 'bahaar Ke Sapne', 'aurat', 'doli' and 'ittefaq' but 'aradhana' in 1969 marked the beginning of 'kaka' in Bollywood
 ‘aradhana’ main rajesh khanna or husn pari sharmila tagore kii jodi ne silver screen par romance or jajbaton kaa wo gajab chithran kiya ki lakhon yuvatiyon kii raaton kii neend udne lagi or ‘kaaka’ prem kaa nayaa pratik ban gaye
 Singers like Kishore Kumar from the film 'aradhana' also got a chance to establish themselves in the Hindi film industry and eventually became the permanent voice of Rajesh Khanna's songs
 rajesh khanna kii bhavuk adaakaari or kishor kii aawaaj ne milakar safalataa ke jhande gaad die
 This melding of performance and voice gave Bollywood classics such as 'mere Sapne Ki Rani', 'roop Tera Mastana', 'kuch toh pehoge kahne', 'jai Jai Shivshankar' and 'zindagi Kaise Hai Paheli'
 ‘aradhana’ or ‘hathi mere saathi’ rajesh khanna kii aisi superhit filmein thim jinhone box aphis par safalataa ke saare puraane record tod die
 He acted in 163 films, out of which 106 films were successful only on his own
 22 filmein aisi thim jinamein unke saath unki takkar ke anya nayak bhi maujuud the
 Rajesh Khanna gave 15 consecutive superhit films between 1969 and 1972
 is record ko aaj tak koi nahin tod paaya he or isi ke baad baliwood main ‘superstar’ kaa aagaaj hua
 He was awarded the Filmfare Award for Best Actor three times for his performance and was nominated for the award 14 times
 varsh 2005 main unhen ‘filmphere lifetime achievement’ puraskaar pradaan kiya gaya
 Despite his romantic image, Rajesh Khanna played a variety of roles, including Anand battling an incurable disease, the cook of 'chef', the lonely husband of 'amar Prem' and the mental patient of 'khamoshi'
 bollywood kaa yah svarnim daur tha or rajesh khanna kii adaakaari ke liye yah sone par suhaaga sabit hua or unhen apane samay ke kala paarkhiyon ke saath kaam karne kaa mauka mila
 Whether he was a film director or actresses and musicians
 ‘amar prem’ or ‘aap kii kasam’ jaisi kai filmon main rajesh khanna kii sharmila tagore or mumtaj ke saath ‘camestry’ aisi match kar gayi ki inhone ek ke baad ek safal filmein deen
 The talent of Rajesh Khanna was further enhanced by Shakti Samanta, Yash Chopra, Manmohan Desai, Rishikesh Mukherjee and Ramesh Sippy
 aar di burman jaisi sangeetkaar or kishor ke saath rajesh khanna ne 30 se adhik filmon main kaam kiya
 Rajesh Khanna's films did not achieve the first success during 1976-78 and after 1978 he acted in films like 'phir Wahi Raat', 'dard', 'dhanwan', 'avatar' and 'agar Tum Na Hote'
 Those who were not successful in terms of earning, but critics definitely appreciated them
 lekin har sitara duubataa he or 80 ke dashak ke uttarardh main box offis par unka jaadu khatm ho gaya
 Rajesh Khanna was a member of the Lok Sabha from 1992 to 1996
 vah congress ke tikat par nayi dilli seat se jite the
 The magic of Rajesh Khanna's personality not only made his fans crazy, but he also played magic on three Bollywood actresses in the heyday
 70 ke dashak main unka anju mahendru ke saath lambey samay tak prem sambandh chalaa
 She later married Dimple Kapadia, 15 years younger to him, in 1973 with whom he has two daughters, Twinkle and Rinke
 dimple kapaadiya 1984 main rajesh khanna se alag ho gayin
 Although they lived separately but never formally divorced
 rajesh khanna kaa ‘sautan’ kii apni nayika tina munim se bhi naam judaa
 The pair gave films like 'fifty Fifty', 'infidelity', 'clue', 'insaaf Main Karega' and 'adhikar'
 jab vah saansad the to unhone apana puraa samay raajnneeti ko diya or abhinay kii peshkashon ko thukraa diya
 He also campaigned for Congress in Punjab in the 2012 general election
 bihar main hue vidhansabha chunaav main bhartiya janata party kii haar se yah bhale hi lag rahaa ho ki pradhanmantri narendra modi kaa jaadu ab chalane vaala nahin he, lekin mulk main vah ab bhi lokapriy hai
 a Pakistani newspaper said this in its editorial on Tuesday
 'da nesan' ne likhaa he ki yah baat dhyaan rakhni chahie ki bihar bharat kaa sirf ek rajya he, or desh ke baaki hisson main modi ab bhi lokapriy hai
